<span data-ttu-id="11607-1620">Dentro de uma função assíncrona, `await` não pode ser usado como um identificador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1620">Inside of an async function, `await` cannot be used as an identifier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1621">Portanto, não há nenhuma ambiguidade sintática entre expressões await e várias expressões que envolvem identificadores.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1621">There is therefore no syntactic ambiguity between await-expressions and various expressions involving identifiers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1622">Fora de funções assíncronas, `await` atua como um identificador normal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1622">Outside of async functions, `await` acts as a normal identifier.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1623">O operando de um *await_expression* é chamado de ***tarefa***.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1623">The operand of an *await_expression* is called the ***task***.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1624">Ele representa uma operação assíncrona que pode ou não pode ser concluída no momento a *await_expression* é avaliada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1624">It represents an asynchronous operation that may or may not be complete at the time the *await_expression* is evaluated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1625">É a finalidade do operador await suspender a execução da função assíncrona até que a tarefa aguardada seja concluída e, em seguida, obter seu resultado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1625">The purpose of the await operator is to suspend execution of the enclosing async function until the awaited task is complete, and then obtain its outcome.</span></span>

#### <a name="awaitable-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="11607-1626">Expressões de awaitable</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1626">Awaitable expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1627">A tarefa de uma expressão await é necessária para ser ***aguardável***.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1627">The task of an await expression is required to be ***awaitable***.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1628">Uma expressão `t` é awaitable, se tiver mantido por um dos seguintes:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1628">An expression `t` is awaitable if one of the following holds:</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1629">`t` é do tipo de tempo de compilação `dynamic`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1629">`t` is of compile time type `dynamic`</span></span>
*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1630">`t` tem um método de extensão ou de instância acessível chamado `GetAwaiter` sem parâmetros e nenhum parâmetro de tipo e um tipo de retorno `A` para o qual todos os itens a seguir manter:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1630">`t` has an accessible instance or extension method called `GetAwaiter` with no parameters and no type parameters, and a return type `A` for which all of the following hold:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="11607-1631">`A` implementa a interface `System.Runtime.CompilerServices.INotifyCompletion` (daqui em diante, conhecido como `INotifyCompletion` para fins de brevidade)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1631">`A` implements the interface `System.Runtime.CompilerServices.INotifyCompletion` (hereafter known as `INotifyCompletion` for brevity)</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="11607-1632">`A` tem uma propriedade de instância acessível e legível `IsCompleted` do tipo `bool`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1632">`A` has an accessible, readable instance property `IsCompleted` of type `bool`</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="11607-1633">`A` tem um método de instância acessível `GetResult` sem parâmetros e nenhum parâmetro de tipo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1633">`A` has an accessible instance method `GetResult` with no parameters and no type parameters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1634">A finalidade de `GetAwaiter` método é obter uma ***awaiter*** para a tarefa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1634">The purpose of the `GetAwaiter` method is to obtain an ***awaiter*** for the task.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1635">O tipo `A` é chamado de ***tipo awaiter*** para a expressão await.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1635">The type `A` is called the ***awaiter type*** for the await expression.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1636">A finalidade de `IsCompleted` é de propriedade determinar se a tarefa já foi concluída.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1636">The purpose of the `IsCompleted` property is to determine if the task is already complete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1637">Nesse caso, não é necessário para suspender a avaliação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1637">If so, there is no need to suspend evaluation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1638">A finalidade do `INotifyCompletion.OnCompleted` método é inscrever-se de "continuação" para a tarefa; ou seja, um delegado (do tipo `System.Action`) que será invocado quando a tarefa for concluída.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1638">The purpose of the `INotifyCompletion.OnCompleted` method is to sign up a "continuation" to the task; i.e. a delegate (of type `System.Action`) that will be invoked once the task is complete.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1639">A finalidade de `GetResult` método é obter o resultado da tarefa quando ela for concluída.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1639">The purpose of the `GetResult` method is to obtain the outcome of the task once it is complete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1640">Esse resultado pode ser a conclusão bem-sucedida, possivelmente com um valor de resultado, ou pode ser uma exceção que é lançada pelo `GetResult` método.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1640">This outcome may be successful completion, possibly with a result value, or it may be an exception which is thrown by the `GetResult` method.</span></span>

#### <a name="classification-of-await-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="11607-1641">Expressões de classificação de await</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1641">Classification of await expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1642">A expressão `await t` é classificado da mesma forma que a expressão `(t).GetAwaiter().GetResult()`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1642">The expression `await t` is classified the same way as the expression `(t).GetAwaiter().GetResult()`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1643">Portanto, se o tipo de retorno de `GetResult` está `void`, o *await_expression* é classificado como nada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1643">Thus, if the return type of `GetResult` is `void`, the *await_expression* is classified as nothing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1644">Se ele tiver um tipo de retorno não nulo `T`, o *await_expression* é classificado como um valor do tipo `T`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1644">If it has a non-void return type `T`, the *await_expression* is classified as a value of type `T`.</span></span>

#### <a name="runtime-evaluation-of-await-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="11607-1645">Expressões de avaliação do tempo de execução do await</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1645">Runtime evaluation of await expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1646">Em tempo de execução, a expressão `await t` é avaliada como segue:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1646">At runtime, the expression `await t` is evaluated as follows:</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1647">Um awaiter `a` é obtido avaliando a expressão `(t).GetAwaiter()`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1647">An awaiter `a` is obtained by evaluating the expression `(t).GetAwaiter()`.</span></span>
*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1648">Um `bool` `b` é obtido avaliando a expressão `(a).IsCompleted`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1648">A `bool` `b` is obtained by evaluating the expression `(a).IsCompleted`.</span></span>
*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1649">Se `b` está `false` e em seguida, avaliação depende `a` implementa a interface `System.Runtime.CompilerServices.ICriticalNotifyCompletion` (daqui em diante, conhecido como `ICriticalNotifyCompletion` para fins de brevidade).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1649">If `b` is `false` then evaluation depends on whether `a` implements the interface `System.Runtime.CompilerServices.ICriticalNotifyCompletion` (hereafter known as `ICriticalNotifyCompletion` for brevity).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1650">Essa verificação é feita no tempo; de ligação ou seja, em tempo de execução se `a` tem o tipo de tempo de compilação `dynamic`e em tempo de compilação caso contrário.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1650">This check is done at binding time; i.e. at runtime if `a` has the compile time type `dynamic`, and at compile time otherwise.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1651">Deixe `r` denotam o delegado de continuação ([iteradores](classes.md#iterators)):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1651">Let `r` denote the resumption delegate ([Iterators](classes.md#iterators)):</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="11607-1652">Se `a` não implementa `ICriticalNotifyCompletion`, em seguida, a expressão `(a as (INotifyCompletion)).OnCompleted(r)` é avaliada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1652">If `a` does not implement `ICriticalNotifyCompletion`, then the expression `(a as (INotifyCompletion)).OnCompleted(r)` is evaluated.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="11607-1653">Se `a` implementar `ICriticalNotifyCompletion`, em seguida, a expressão `(a as (ICriticalNotifyCompletion)).UnsafeOnCompleted(r)` é avaliada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1653">If `a` does implement `ICriticalNotifyCompletion`, then the expression `(a as (ICriticalNotifyCompletion)).UnsafeOnCompleted(r)` is evaluated.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="11607-1654">Avaliação, em seguida, é suspenso e controle é retornado ao chamador da função assíncrona atual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1654">Evaluation is then suspended, and control is returned to the current caller of the async function.</span></span>
*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1655">Qualquer um dos imediatamente após (se `b` foi `true`), ou mediante posterior invocação de delegado de continuação (se `b` foi `false`), a expressão `(a).GetResult()` é avaliada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1655">Either immediately after (if `b` was `true`), or upon later invocation of the resumption delegate (if `b` was `false`), the expression `(a).GetResult()` is evaluated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1656">Se ela retorna um valor, esse valor é o resultado do *await_expression*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1656">If it returns a value, that value is the result of the *await_expression*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1657">Caso contrário, o resultado é que nada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1657">Otherwise the result is nothing.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1658">A implementação de um awaiter métodos da interface `INotifyCompletion.OnCompleted` e `ICriticalNotifyCompletion.UnsafeOnCompleted` deve fazer com que o delegado `r` a ser invocado no máximo uma vez.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1658">An awaiter's implementation of the interface methods `INotifyCompletion.OnCompleted` and `ICriticalNotifyCompletion.UnsafeOnCompleted` should cause the delegate `r` to be invoked at most once.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1659">Caso contrário, o comportamento da função async será indefinido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1659">Otherwise, the behavior of the enclosing async function is undefined.</span></span>

## <a name="arithmetic-operators"></a><span data-ttu-id="11607-1660">Operadores aritméticos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1660">Arithmetic operators</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1661">O `*`, `/`, `%`, `+`, e `-` operadores são chamados de operadores aritméticos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1661">The `*`, `/`, `%`, `+`, and `-` operators are called the arithmetic operators.</span></span>

```antlr
multiplicative_expression
    : unary_expression
    | multiplicative_expression '*' unary_expression
    | multiplicative_expression '/' unary_expression
    | multiplicative_expression '%' unary_expression
    ;

additive_expression
    : multiplicative_expression
    | additive_expression '+' multiplicative_expression
    | additive_expression '-' multiplicative_expression
    ;
```

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1662">Se um operando do operador aritmético tem o tipo de tempo de compilação `dynamic`, em seguida, a expressão está associada dinamicamente ([vinculação dinâmica](expressions.md#dynamic-binding)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1662">If an operand of an arithmetic operator has the compile-time type `dynamic`, then the expression is dynamically bound ([Dynamic binding](expressions.md#dynamic-binding)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1663">Nesse caso é o tipo de tempo de compilação da expressão `dynamic`, e a resolução descrita a seguir ocorrerá em tempo de execução usando o tipo de tempo de execução desses operandos que tenham o tipo de tempo de compilação `dynamic`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1663">In this case the compile-time type of the expression is `dynamic`, and the resolution described below will take place at run-time using the run-time type of those operands that have the compile-time type `dynamic`.</span></span>

### <a name="multiplication-operator"></a><span data-ttu-id="11607-1664">Operador de multiplicação</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1664">Multiplication operator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1665">Para uma operação do formulário `x * y`, resolução de sobrecarga de operador binário ([resolução de sobrecarga de operador binário](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) é aplicado para selecionar uma implementação do operador específico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1665">For an operation of the form `x * y`, binary operator overload resolution ([Binary operator overload resolution](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) is applied to select a specific operator implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1666">Os operandos são convertidos nos tipos de parâmetro do operador selecionado e o tipo do resultado é o tipo de retorno do operador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1666">The operands are converted to the parameter types of the selected operator, and the type of the result is the return type of the operator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1667">Os operadores de multiplicação predefinidos estão listados abaixo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1667">The predefined multiplication operators are listed below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1668">Todos os operadores compute o produto dos `x` e `y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1668">The operators all compute the product of `x` and `y`.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1669">Multiplicação de inteiro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1669">Integer multiplication:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   int operator *(int x, int y);
   uint operator *(uint x, uint y);
   long operator *(long x, long y);
   ulong operator *(ulong x, ulong y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1670">Em um `checked` contexto, se o produto está fora do intervalo do tipo de resultado, um `System.OverflowException` é gerada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1670">In a `checked` context, if the product is outside the range of the result type, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1671">Em um `unchecked` contexto, estouros não são relatados e quaisquer bits de ordem superior significativos fora do intervalo do tipo de resultado são descartados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1671">In an `unchecked` context, overflows are not reported and any significant high-order bits outside the range of the result type are discarded.</span></span>


*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1672">Multiplicação de ponto flutuante:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1672">Floating-point multiplication:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   float operator *(float x, float y);
   double operator *(double x, double y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1673">O produto é calculado de acordo com as regras de aritmética do IEEE 754.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1673">The product is computed according to the rules of IEEE 754 arithmetic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1674">A tabela a seguir lista os resultados de todas as combinações possíveis de valores Finitas diferente de zero, zeros, infinitos e do NaN.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1674">The following table lists the results of all possible combinations of nonzero finite values, zeros, infinities, and NaN's.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1675">Na tabela, `x` e `y` são valores positivos de finitos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1675">In the table, `x` and `y` are positive finite values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1676">`z` é o resultado de `x * y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1676">`z` is the result of `x * y`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1677">Se o resultado for muito grande para o tipo de destino, `z` é infinito.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1677">If the result is too large for the destination type, `z` is infinity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1678">Se o resultado for muito pequeno para o tipo de destino, `z` é zero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1678">If the result is too small for the destination type, `z` is zero.</span></span>

   |      |      |      |     |     |      |      |     |
   |:----:|-----:|:----:|:---:|:---:|:----:|:----:|:----|
   |      | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1679">+y</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1679">+y</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1680">-y</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1680">-y</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1681">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1681">+0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1682">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1682">-0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1683">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1683">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1684">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1684">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1685">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1685">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1686">+x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1686">+x</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1687">+z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1687">+z</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1688">-z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1688">-z</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1689">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1689">+0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1690">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1690">-0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1691">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1691">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1692">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1692">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1693">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1693">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1694">-x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1694">-x</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1695">-z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1695">-z</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1696">+z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1696">+z</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1697">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1697">-0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1698">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1698">+0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1699">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1699">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1700">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1700">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1701">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1701">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1702">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1702">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1703">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1703">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1704">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1704">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1705">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1705">+0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1706">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1706">-0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1707">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1707">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1708">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1708">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1709">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1709">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1710">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1710">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1711">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1711">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1712">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1712">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1713">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1713">-0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1714">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1714">+0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1715">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1715">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1716">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1716">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1717">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1717">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1718">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1718">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1719">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1719">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1720">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1720">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1721">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1721">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1722">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1722">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1723">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1723">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1724">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1724">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1725">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1725">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1726">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1726">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1727">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1727">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1728">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1728">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1729">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1729">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1730">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1730">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1731">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1731">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1732">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1732">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1733">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1733">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1734">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1734">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1735">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1735">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1736">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1736">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1737">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1737">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1738">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1738">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1739">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1739">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1740">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1740">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1741">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1741">NaN</span></span> | 

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1742">Multiplicação decimal:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1742">Decimal multiplication:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   decimal operator *(decimal x, decimal y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1743">Se o valor resultante é muito grande para representar o `decimal` formato, um `System.OverflowException` é gerada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1743">If the resulting value is too large to represent in the `decimal` format, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1744">Se o valor do resultado for muito pequeno para representar o `decimal` formato, o resultado é zero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1744">If the result value is too small to represent in the `decimal` format, the result is zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1745">A escala do resultado, antes de qualquer arredondamento, é a soma das escalas dos dois operandos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1745">The scale of the result, before any rounding, is the sum of the scales of the two operands.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1746">Multiplicação decimal é equivalente a usar o operador de multiplicação do tipo `System.Decimal`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1746">Decimal multiplication is equivalent to using the multiplication operator of type `System.Decimal`.</span></span>


### <a name="division-operator"></a><span data-ttu-id="11607-1747">Operador de divisão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1747">Division operator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1748">Para uma operação do formulário `x / y`, resolução de sobrecarga de operador binário ([resolução de sobrecarga de operador binário](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) é aplicado para selecionar uma implementação do operador específico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1748">For an operation of the form `x / y`, binary operator overload resolution ([Binary operator overload resolution](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) is applied to select a specific operator implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1749">Os operandos são convertidos nos tipos de parâmetro do operador selecionado e o tipo do resultado é o tipo de retorno do operador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1749">The operands are converted to the parameter types of the selected operator, and the type of the result is the return type of the operator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1750">Os operadores de divisão predefinidos estão listados abaixo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1750">The predefined division operators are listed below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1751">O quociente de computação de todos os operadores `x` e `y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1751">The operators all compute the quotient of `x` and `y`.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1752">Divisão de inteiros:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1752">Integer division:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   int operator /(int x, int y);
   uint operator /(uint x, uint y);
   long operator /(long x, long y);
   ulong operator /(ulong x, ulong y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1753">Se o valor do operando à direita for zero, um `System.DivideByZeroException` é gerada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1753">If the value of the right operand is zero, a `System.DivideByZeroException` is thrown.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1754">A divisão Arredonda o resultado em direção a zero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1754">The division rounds the result towards zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1755">Assim, o valor absoluto do resultado é o maior inteiro possível que seja menor ou igual ao valor absoluto do quociente de dois operandos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1755">Thus the absolute value of the result is the largest possible integer that is less than or equal to the absolute value of the quotient of the two operands.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1756">O resultado é zero ou positivo quando os dois operandos têm o mesmo sinal e zero ou negativo quando os dois operandos tiverem oposta sinais.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1756">The result is zero or positive when the two operands have the same sign and zero or negative when the two operands have opposite signs.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1757">Se o operando esquerdo for menor representável `int` ou `long` valor e o operando direito é `-1`, ocorre um estouro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1757">If the left operand is the smallest representable `int` or `long` value and the right operand is `-1`, an overflow occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1758">Em um `checked` contexto, isso faz com que um `System.ArithmeticException` (ou uma subclasse disso) seja lançada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1758">In a `checked` context, this causes a `System.ArithmeticException` (or a subclass thereof) to be thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1759">Em um `unchecked` contexto, ele é definido pela implementação sobre se um `System.ArithmeticException` (ou uma subclasse disso) é gerada ou o estouro é relatado com o valor resultante, sendo que a do operando à esquerda.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1759">In an `unchecked` context, it is implementation-defined as to whether a `System.ArithmeticException` (or a subclass thereof) is thrown or the overflow goes unreported with the resulting value being that of the left operand.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1760">Divisão de ponto flutuante:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1760">Floating-point division:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   float operator /(float x, float y);
   double operator /(double x, double y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1761">O quociente é calculado de acordo com as regras de aritmética do IEEE 754.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1761">The quotient is computed according to the rules of IEEE 754 arithmetic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1762">A tabela a seguir lista os resultados de todas as combinações possíveis de valores Finitas diferente de zero, zeros, infinitos e do NaN.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1762">The following table lists the results of all possible combinations of nonzero finite values, zeros, infinities, and NaN's.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1763">Na tabela, `x` e `y` são valores positivos de finitos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1763">In the table, `x` and `y` are positive finite values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1764">`z` é o resultado de `x / y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1764">`z` is the result of `x / y`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1765">Se o resultado for muito grande para o tipo de destino, `z` é infinito.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1765">If the result is too large for the destination type, `z` is infinity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1766">Se o resultado for muito pequeno para o tipo de destino, `z` é zero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1766">If the result is too small for the destination type, `z` is zero.</span></span>

   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1790">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1790">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1791">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1791">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1792">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1792">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1793">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1793">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1794">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1794">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1795">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1795">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1796">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1796">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1797">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1797">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1798">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1798">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1799">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1799">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1800">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1800">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1801">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1801">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1802">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1802">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1803">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1803">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1804">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1804">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1805">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1805">NaN</span></span>  |

   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1814">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1814">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1815">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1815">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1816">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1816">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1817">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1817">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1818">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1818">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1819">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1819">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1820">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1820">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1821">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1821">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1822">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1822">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1823">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1823">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1824">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1824">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1825">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1825">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1826">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1826">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1827">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1827">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1828">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1828">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1829">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1829">NaN</span></span>  | 

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1830">Divisão decimal:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1830">Decimal division:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   decimal operator /(decimal x, decimal y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1831">Se o valor do operando à direita for zero, um `System.DivideByZeroException` é gerada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1831">If the value of the right operand is zero, a `System.DivideByZeroException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1832">Se o valor resultante é muito grande para representar o `decimal` formato, um `System.OverflowException` é gerada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1832">If the resulting value is too large to represent in the `decimal` format, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1833">Se o valor do resultado for muito pequeno para representar o `decimal` formato, o resultado é zero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1833">If the result value is too small to represent in the `decimal` format, the result is zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1834">A escala do resultado é a escala menor que irá preservar um resultado igual ao valor decimal representável para o resultado matemático true mais próximo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1834">The scale of the result is the smallest scale that will preserve a result equal to the nearest representable decimal value to the true mathematical result.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1835">Divisão decimal é equivalente a usar o operador de divisão do tipo `System.Decimal`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1835">Decimal division is equivalent to using the division operator of type `System.Decimal`.</span></span>


### <a name="remainder-operator"></a><span data-ttu-id="11607-1836">Operador restante</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1836">Remainder operator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1837">Para uma operação do formulário `x % y`, resolução de sobrecarga de operador binário ([resolução de sobrecarga de operador binário](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) é aplicado para selecionar uma implementação do operador específico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1837">For an operation of the form `x % y`, binary operator overload resolution ([Binary operator overload resolution](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) is applied to select a specific operator implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1838">Os operandos são convertidos nos tipos de parâmetro do operador selecionado e o tipo do resultado é o tipo de retorno do operador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1838">The operands are converted to the parameter types of the selected operator, and the type of the result is the return type of the operator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1839">Os operadores de restante predefinidos estão listados abaixo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1839">The predefined remainder operators are listed below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1840">Todos os operadores compute o resto da divisão entre `x` e `y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1840">The operators all compute the remainder of the division between `x` and `y`.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1841">Resto inteiro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1841">Integer remainder:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   int operator %(int x, int y);
   uint operator %(uint x, uint y);
   long operator %(long x, long y);
   ulong operator %(ulong x, ulong y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1842">O resultado de `x % y` é o valor produzido por `x - (x / y) * y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1842">The result of `x % y` is the value produced by `x - (x / y) * y`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1843">Se `y` for zero, um `System.DivideByZeroException` é gerada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1843">If `y` is zero, a `System.DivideByZeroException` is thrown.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1844">Se o operando esquerdo for menor `int` ou `long` é de valor e o operando direito `-1`, um `System.OverflowException` é gerada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1844">If the left operand is the smallest `int` or `long` value and the right operand is `-1`, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1845">Em nenhum caso faz `x % y` lançar uma exceção onde `x / y` não geraria uma exceção.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1845">In no case does `x % y` throw an exception where `x / y` would not throw an exception.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1846">Ponto flutuante restante:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1846">Floating-point remainder:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   float operator %(float x, float y);
   double operator %(double x, double y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1847">A tabela a seguir lista os resultados de todas as combinações possíveis de valores Finitas diferente de zero, zeros, infinitos e do NaN.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1847">The following table lists the results of all possible combinations of nonzero finite values, zeros, infinities, and NaN's.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1848">Na tabela, `x` e `y` são valores positivos de finitos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1848">In the table, `x` and `y` are positive finite values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1849">`z` é o resultado de `x % y` e é computado como `x - n * y`, onde `n` é o maior inteiro possíveis que é menor que ou igual a `x / y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1849">`z` is the result of `x % y` and is computed as `x - n * y`, where `n` is the largest possible integer that is less than or equal to `x / y`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1850">Esse método de computação o restante é análogo àquela utilizada para operandos de inteiro, mas é diferente da definição de IEEE 754 (no qual `n` é o inteiro mais próximo ao `x / y`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1850">This method of computing the remainder is analogous to that used for integer operands, but differs from the IEEE 754 definition (in which `n` is the integer closest to `x / y`).</span></span>

   |:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|
   |      | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1851">+y</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1851">+y</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1852">-y</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1852">-y</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1853">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1853">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1854">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1854">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1855">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1855">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1856">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1856">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1857">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1857">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1858">+x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1858">+x</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1859">+z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1859">+z</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1860">+z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1860">+z</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1861">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1861">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1862">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1862">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1863">x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1863">x</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1864">x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1864">x</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1865">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1865">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1866">-x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1866">-x</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1867">-z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1867">-z</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1868">-z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1868">-z</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1869">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1869">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1870">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1870">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1871">-x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1871">-x</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1872">-x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1872">-x</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1873">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1873">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1874">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1874">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1875">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1875">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1876">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1876">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1877">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1877">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1878">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1878">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1879">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1879">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1880">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1880">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1881">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1881">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1882">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1882">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1883">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1883">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1884">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1884">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1885">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1885">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1886">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1886">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1887">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1887">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1888">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1888">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1889">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1889">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1890">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1890">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1891">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1891">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1892">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1892">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1893">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1893">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1894">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1894">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1895">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1895">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1896">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1896">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1897">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1897">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1898">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1898">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1899">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1899">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1900">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1900">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1901">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1901">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1902">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1902">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1903">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1903">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1904">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1904">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1905">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1905">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1906">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1906">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1907">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1907">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1908">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1908">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1909">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1909">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1910">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1910">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1911">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1911">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1912">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1912">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1913">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1913">NaN</span></span>  | 

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1914">Decimal restante:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1914">Decimal remainder:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   decimal operator %(decimal x, decimal y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1915">Se o valor do operando à direita for zero, um `System.DivideByZeroException` é gerada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1915">If the value of the right operand is zero, a `System.DivideByZeroException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1916">A escala do resultado, antes de qualquer arredondamento, é o maior entre as escalas de dois operandos, e o sinal do resultado, se diferente de zero, é o mesmo da `x`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1916">The scale of the result, before any rounding, is the larger of the scales of the two operands, and the sign of the result, if non-zero, is the same as that of `x`.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1917">Decimal restante é equivalente a usar o operador de resto do tipo `System.Decimal`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1917">Decimal remainder is equivalent to using the remainder operator of type `System.Decimal`.</span></span>


### <a name="addition-operator"></a><span data-ttu-id="11607-1918">Operador de adição</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1918">Addition operator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1919">Para uma operação do formulário `x + y`, resolução de sobrecarga de operador binário ([resolução de sobrecarga de operador binário](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) é aplicado para selecionar uma implementação do operador específico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1919">For an operation of the form `x + y`, binary operator overload resolution ([Binary operator overload resolution](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) is applied to select a specific operator implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1920">Os operandos são convertidos nos tipos de parâmetro do operador selecionado e o tipo do resultado é o tipo de retorno do operador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1920">The operands are converted to the parameter types of the selected operator, and the type of the result is the return type of the operator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-1921">Os operadores de adição predefinidas são listados abaixo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1921">The predefined addition operators are listed below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1922">Para tipos numéricos e de enumeração, os operadores de adição predefinidos calcular a soma dos dois operandos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1922">For numeric and enumeration types, the predefined addition operators compute the sum of the two operands.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1923">Quando um ou ambos os operandos são do tipo cadeia de caracteres, os operadores de adição predefinidos concatenar a representação de cadeia de caracteres dos operandos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1923">When one or both operands are of type string, the predefined addition operators concatenate the string representation of the operands.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1924">Adição de inteiro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1924">Integer addition:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   int operator +(int x, int y);
   uint operator +(uint x, uint y);
   long operator +(long x, long y);
   ulong operator +(ulong x, ulong y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1925">Em um `checked` contexto, se a soma está fora do intervalo do tipo de resultado, um `System.OverflowException` é gerada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1925">In a `checked` context, if the sum is outside the range of the result type, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1926">Em um `unchecked` contexto, estouros não são relatados e quaisquer bits de ordem superior significativos fora do intervalo do tipo de resultado são descartados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1926">In an `unchecked` context, overflows are not reported and any significant high-order bits outside the range of the result type are discarded.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1927">Adição de ponto flutuante:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1927">Floating-point addition:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   float operator +(float x, float y);
   double operator +(double x, double y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1928">A soma é calculada de acordo com as regras de aritmética do IEEE 754.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1928">The sum is computed according to the rules of IEEE 754 arithmetic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1929">A tabela a seguir lista os resultados de todas as combinações possíveis de valores Finitas diferente de zero, zeros, infinitos e do NaN.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1929">The following table lists the results of all possible combinations of nonzero finite values, zeros, infinities, and NaN's.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1930">Na tabela, `x` e `y` são valores Finitas diferente de zero, e `z` é o resultado de `x + y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1930">In the table, `x` and `y` are nonzero finite values, and `z` is the result of `x + y`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1931">Se `x` e `y` têm a mesma magnitude mas oposta sinais, `z` for zero positivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1931">If `x` and `y` have the same magnitude but opposite signs, `z` is positive zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1932">Se `x + y` é muito grande para ser representado no tipo de destino, `z` é infinito com o mesmo sinal que `x + y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1932">If `x + y` is too large to represent in the destination type, `z` is an infinity with the same sign as `x + y`.</span></span>

   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1953">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1953">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1954">y</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1954">y</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1955">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1955">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1956">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1956">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1957">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1957">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1958">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1958">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1959">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1959">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1960">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1960">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1961">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1961">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1962">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1962">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1963">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1963">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1964">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1964">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1965">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1965">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1966">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1966">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1967">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1967">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1968">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1968">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1969">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1969">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1970">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1970">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1971">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1971">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1972">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1972">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1973">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1973">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1974">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1974">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1975">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1975">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1976">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1976">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1977">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1977">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1978">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1978">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1979">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1979">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-1980">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1980">NaN</span></span>  | 

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1981">Adição de decimal:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1981">Decimal addition:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   decimal operator +(decimal x, decimal y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1982">Se o valor resultante é muito grande para representar o `decimal` formato, um `System.OverflowException` é gerada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1982">If the resulting value is too large to represent in the `decimal` format, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1983">A escala do resultado, antes de qualquer arredondamento, é o maior entre as escalas de dois operandos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1983">The scale of the result, before any rounding, is the larger of the scales of the two operands.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1984">Adição de decimal é equivalente a usar o operador de adição do tipo `System.Decimal`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1984">Decimal addition is equivalent to using the addition operator of type `System.Decimal`.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1985">Adição de enumeração.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1985">Enumeration addition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1986">Implicitamente, a cada tipo de enumeração fornece o seguinte predefinidas operadores, onde `E` é o tipo de enumeração, e `U` é o tipo subjacente de `E`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1986">Every enumeration type implicitly provides the following predefined operators, where `E` is the enum type, and `U` is the underlying type of `E`:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   E operator +(E x, U y);
   E operator +(U x, E y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1987">Em tempo de execução, esses operadores são avaliados exatamente como `(E)((U)x + (U)y)`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1987">At run-time these operators are evaluated exactly as `(E)((U)x + (U)y)`.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1988">Concatenação de cadeia de caracteres:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1988">String concatenation:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   string operator +(string x, string y);
   string operator +(string x, object y);
   string operator +(object x, string y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1989">Essas sobrecargas do binário `+` operador realizam a concatenação de cadeia de caracteres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1989">These overloads of the binary `+` operator perform string concatenation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1990">Se um operando de concatenação de cadeia de caracteres é `null`, uma cadeia de caracteres vazia é substituída.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1990">If an operand of string concatenation is `null`, an empty string is substituted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1991">Caso contrário, qualquer argumento de cadeia de caracteres não é convertido em sua representação de cadeia de caracteres com a invocação virtual `ToString` método herdado do tipo `object`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1991">Otherwise, any non-string argument is converted to its string representation by invoking the virtual `ToString` method inherited from type `object`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1992">Se `ToString` retorna `null`, uma cadeia de caracteres vazia é substituída.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1992">If `ToString` returns `null`, an empty string is substituted.</span></span>

   ```csharp
   using System;
   
   class Test
   {
       static void Main() {
           string s = null;
           Console.WriteLine("s = >" + s + "<");        // displays s = ><
           int i = 1;
           Console.WriteLine("i = " + i);               // displays i = 1
           float f = 1.2300E+15F;
           Console.WriteLine("f = " + f);               // displays f = 1.23E+15
           decimal d = 2.900m;
           Console.WriteLine("d = " + d);               // displays d = 2.900
       }
   }
   ```

   O resultado do operador de concatenação de cadeia de caracteres é uma cadeia de caracteres que consiste em caracteres do operando à esquerda seguido pelos caracteres do operando à direita. O operador de concatenação de cadeia de caracteres nunca retorna um `null` valor. <span data-ttu-id="11607-1995">Um `System.OutOfMemoryException` poderá ser gerada se não há memória suficiente disponível para alocar a cadeia de caracteres resultante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1995">A `System.OutOfMemoryException` may be thrown if there is not enough memory available to allocate the resulting string.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-1996">Combinação de delegado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1996">Delegate combination.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1997">Cada tipo de delegado implicitamente fornece o operador pré-definido seguinte, onde `D` é o tipo de delegado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1997">Every delegate type implicitly provides the following predefined operator, where `D` is the delegate type:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   D operator +(D x, D y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-1998">O binário `+` operador executa a combinação de delegados quando ambos os operandos são de algum tipo de delegado `D`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1998">The binary `+` operator performs delegate combination when both operands are of some delegate type `D`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-1999">(Se os operandos tiverem tipos diferentes de delegado, ocorrerá um erro em tempo de associação.) Se for o primeiro operando `null`, o resultado da operação é o valor do segundo operando (mesmo que seja também `null`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-1999">(If the operands have different delegate types, a binding-time error occurs.) If the first operand is `null`, the result of the operation is the value of the second operand (even if that is also `null`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-2000">Caso contrário, se o segundo operando for `null`, o resultado da operação será o valor do primeiro operando.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2000">Otherwise, if the second operand is `null`, then the result of the operation is the value of the first operand.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-2001">Caso contrário, o resultado da operação é uma nova instância delegada que, quando invocado, invoca o primeiro operando e, em seguida, invoca o segundo operando.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2001">Otherwise, the result of the operation is a new delegate instance that, when invoked, invokes the first operand and then invokes the second operand.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-2002">Para obter exemplos de combinação de delegados, consulte [operador de subtração](expressions.md#subtraction-operator) e [invocação de delegado](delegates.md#delegate-invocation).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2002">For examples of delegate combination, see [Subtraction operator](expressions.md#subtraction-operator) and [Delegate invocation](delegates.md#delegate-invocation).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-2003">Uma vez que `System.Delegate` não é um tipo de delegado `operator`  `+` não está definido para ele.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2003">Since `System.Delegate` is not a delegate type, `operator` `+` is not defined for it.</span></span>

### <a name="subtraction-operator"></a><span data-ttu-id="11607-2004">Operador de subtração</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2004">Subtraction operator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-2005">Para uma operação do formulário `x - y`, resolução de sobrecarga de operador binário ([resolução de sobrecarga de operador binário](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) é aplicado para selecionar uma implementação do operador específico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2005">For an operation of the form `x - y`, binary operator overload resolution ([Binary operator overload resolution](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) is applied to select a specific operator implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-2006">Os operandos são convertidos nos tipos de parâmetro do operador selecionado e o tipo do resultado é o tipo de retorno do operador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2006">The operands are converted to the parameter types of the selected operator, and the type of the result is the return type of the operator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="11607-2007">Os operadores de subtração predefinidas são listados abaixo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2007">The predefined subtraction operators are listed below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-2008">Os operadores todos subtrair `y` de `x`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2008">The operators all subtract `y` from `x`.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-2009">Subtração de inteiro:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2009">Integer subtraction:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   int operator -(int x, int y);
   uint operator -(uint x, uint y);
   long operator -(long x, long y);
   ulong operator -(ulong x, ulong y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-2010">Em um `checked` contexto, se a diferença está fora do intervalo do tipo de resultado, um `System.OverflowException` é gerada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2010">In a `checked` context, if the difference is outside the range of the result type, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-2011">Em um `unchecked` contexto, estouros não são relatados e quaisquer bits de ordem superior significativos fora do intervalo do tipo de resultado são descartados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2011">In an `unchecked` context, overflows are not reported and any significant high-order bits outside the range of the result type are discarded.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-2012">Subtração de ponto flutuante:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2012">Floating-point subtraction:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   float operator -(float x, float y);
   double operator -(double x, double y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="11607-2013">A diferença é calculada de acordo com as regras de aritmética do IEEE 754.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2013">The difference is computed according to the rules of IEEE 754 arithmetic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-2014">A tabela a seguir lista os resultados de todas as combinações possíveis de valores Finitas diferente de zero, zeros, infinitos e NaNs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2014">The following table lists the results of all possible combinations of nonzero finite values, zeros, infinities, and NaNs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-2015">Na tabela, `x` e `y` são valores Finitas diferente de zero, e `z` é o resultado de `x - y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2015">In the table, `x` and `y` are nonzero finite values, and `z` is the result of `x - y`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-2016">Se `x` e `y` forem iguais, `z` for zero positivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2016">If `x` and `y` are equal, `z` is positive zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="11607-2017">Se `x - y` é muito grande para ser representado no tipo de destino, `z` é infinito com o mesmo sinal que `x - y`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2017">If `x - y` is too large to represent in the destination type, `z` is an infinity with the same sign as `x - y`.</span></span>

   |      |      |      |      |      |      |     |
   |:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:---:|
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2018">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2018">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2019">y</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2019">y</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2020">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2020">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2021">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2021">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2022">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2022">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2023">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2023">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2024">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2024">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2025">x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2025">x</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2026">z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2026">z</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2027">x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2027">x</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2028">x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2028">x</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2029">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2029">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2030">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2030">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2031">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2031">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2032">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2032">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2033">-y</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2033">-y</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2034">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2034">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2035">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2035">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2036">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2036">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2037">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2037">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2038">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2038">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2039">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2039">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2040">-y</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2040">-y</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2041">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2041">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2042">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2042">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2043">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2043">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2044">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2044">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2045">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2045">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2046">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2046">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2047">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2047">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2048">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2048">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2049">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2049">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2050">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2050">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2051">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2051">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2052">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2052">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2053">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2053">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2054">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2054">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2055">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2055">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2056">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2056">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2057">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2057">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2058">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2058">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2059">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2059">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2060">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2060">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2061">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2061">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2062">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2062">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2063">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2063">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2064">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2064">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2065">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2065">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="11607-2066">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2066">NaN</span></span> | 

*  <span data-ttu-id="11607-2067">Subtração decimal:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="11607-2067">Decimal subtraction:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   decimal operator -(decimal x, decimal y);
   ```
